DROP TABLE hexdata;
CREATE TABLE hexdata(
  HEX_TERRAIN VARCHAR(1) NOT NULL
, HEX_N_TERRAIN VARCHAR(1) NOT NULL
, HEX_NE_TERRAIN VARCHAR(1) NOT NULL
, HEX_SE_TERRAIN VARCHAR(1) NOT NULL
, HEX_S_TERRAIN VARCHAR(1) NOT NULL
, HEX_SW_TERRAIN VARCHAR(1) NOT NULL
, HEX_NW_TERRAIN VARCHAR(1) NOT NULL
, HEX_BUILDING INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_OIL INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_FARM INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_MILL INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_RIG INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_GOLD INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_NEW_COMBAT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_BATTLE_FOUGHT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_N_CONTROL INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_NE_CONTROL INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_SE_CONTROL INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_S_CONTROL INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_SW_CONTROL INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEX_NW_CONTROL INTEGER  NOT NULL
, FIELD22 INTEGER  NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE basedata(
  BASE_NAME VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL
, BASE_HEX INTEGER  NOT NULL
, BASE_FACTION INTEGER  NOT NULL
, BASE_TIER INTEGER  NOT NULL
, BASE_GOLD INTEGER  NOT NULL
, BASE_LUMBER INTEGER  NOT NULL
, BASE_OIL INTEGER  NOT NULL
, BASE_ALIVE BIT  NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE buildables(
  GRUNT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, BERSERKER INTEGER  NOT NULL
, AXETHROWER INTEGER  NOT NULL
, OGRE INTEGER  NOT NULL
, CATAPULT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, DEATH_KNIGHT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, WAVE_RIDER INTEGER  NOT NULL
, TURTLE INTEGER  NOT NULL
, JUGGERNAUT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HORDE_TRANSPORT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, DRAGON INTEGER  NOT NULL
, RAIDER INTEGER  NOT NULL
, SHAMAN INTEGER  NOT NULL
, WARLOCK INTEGER  NOT NULL
, FOOTMAN INTEGER  NOT NULL
, ARCHER INTEGER  NOT NULL
, KNIGHT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, BALLISTA INTEGER  NOT NULL
, MAGE INTEGER  NOT NULL
, DESTROYER INTEGER  NOT NULL
, SUBMARINE INTEGER  NOT NULL
, BATTLESHIP INTEGER  NOT NULL
, ALLIANCE_TRANSPORT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, GRYPHON INTEGER  NOT NULL
, DWARF INTEGER  NOT NULL
, SWORDSMAN INTEGER  NOT NULL
, WILDHAMMER_SHAMAN INTEGER  NOT NULL
, ROGUE INTEGER  NOT NULL
, SKELETON INTEGER  NOT NULL
, DEMON INTEGER  NOT NULL
, ELEMENTAL INTEGER  NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE unitstats(
  NAME VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL
, MAX_HP INTEGER  NOT NULL
, COMBAT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, CATEGORY INTEGER  NOT NULL
, TYPE INTEGER  NOT NULL
, LIGHT_ARMOR INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HEAVY_ARMOR INTEGER  NOT NULL
, NATURAL_ARMOR INTEGER  NOT NULL
, MOVEMENT INTEGER  NOT NULL
, VISION INTEGER  NOT NULL
, GOLD_COST INTEGER  NOT NULL
, LUMBER_COST INTEGER  NOT NULL
, OIL_COST INTEGER  NOT NULL
, MIN_TIER INTEGER  NOT NULL

CREATE TABLE unitdata(
  NAME VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL
, FACTION INTEGER  NOT NULL
, HIT_POINTS INTEGER  NOT NULL
, LOCATION INTEGER  NOT NULL
, TIER INTEGER  NOT NULL
, TIER_1 VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL
, TIER_2 VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL
, TIER_3 VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL
, TIER_4 VARCHAR(4) NOT NULL
, ALIVE INTEGER  NOT NULL
);
